[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m     # Helper function to merge tiles in a row towards left (or up)
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m     def merge(row):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m         i = 0
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m         j = 1
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m         while j < len(row):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m             if row[i] == 0 and row[j] != 0:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m                 # Move the non-zero tile left
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m                 row[i], row[j] = row[j], row[i]
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m                 j += 1
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m             elif row[i] != 0 and row[i] == row[j]:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m                 # Merge tiles
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m                 row[i] *= 2
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m                 row[j] = 0
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m                 i = j + 1
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m                 j += 1
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m             else:
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m                 i += 1
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m                 j += 1
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m         return row

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m             for i in range(4):
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m                 board[i] = merge(board[i])
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401359)[0m         elif direction == "S":

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401363)[0m     def merge(board, row, direction='W'):

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401361)[0m                 best_score = score
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401361)[0m                 best_move = move

[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401361)[0m                 board[row][col] = stack[row]
[36m(RewardLoopWorker pid=401361)[0m         return board, get_score(board)
